LLM-Safety Evaluations Lack Robustness
Authors: Tim Beyer, Sophie Xhonneux, Simon Geisler, Gauthier Gidel, Leo Schwinn, Stephan Günnemann
First: 2025-03-04T12:55:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-18T17:54:05+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
In this paper, we argue that current safety alignment research efforts for large language models are hindered by many intertwined sources of noise, such as small datasets, methodological inconsistencies, and unreliable evaluation setups. This can, at times, make it impossible to evaluate and compare attacks and defenses fairly, thereby slowing progress. We systematically analyze the LLM safety evaluation pipeline, covering dataset curation, optimization strategies for automated red-teaming, response generation, and response evaluation using LLM judges. At each stage, we identify key issues and highlight their practical impact. We also propose a set of guidelines for reducing noise and bias in evaluations of future attack and defense papers. Lastly, we offer an opposing perspective, highlighting practical reasons for existing limitations. We believe that addressing the outlined problems in future research will improve the field's ability to generate easily comparable results and make measurable progress.
中文标题/摘要
标题：大型语言模型安全评估缺乏稳健性
在本文中，我们认为当前针对大型语言模型的安全对齐研究受到许多交织的噪声源的阻碍，例如小数据集、方法不一致和不可靠的评估设置。这有时使得公平评估和比较攻击与防御变得不可能，从而减缓进展。我们系统分析了LLM安全评估流程，涵盖数据集策划、自动红队的优化策略、响应生成和使用LLM评审的响应评估。在每个阶段，我们识别关键问题并强调其实际影响。我们还提出了一套减少未来攻击和防御论文评估中的噪声和偏见的指导方针。最后，我们提供了一个对立的观点，强调现有限制的实际原因。我们相信，解决未来研究中概述的问题将提高该领域生成易于比较结果和实现可测量进展的能力。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenges faced in safety alignment for large language models (LLMs), particularly the noise from small datasets, methodological inconsistencies, and unreliable evaluation setups that hinder fair comparisons of attacks and defenses. Previous methods have struggled with these issues, leading to slow progress in the field. The proposed approach systematically analyzes the LLM safety evaluation pipeline and identifies key problems at each stage, offering guidelines to reduce noise and bias in future evaluations. This contribution aims to enhance the comparability of results and facilitate measurable advancements in LLM safety research. The methodology includes a comprehensive examination of dataset curation, optimization strategies for automated red-teaming, response generation, and evaluation using LLM judges, ultimately supporting the goal of improving evaluation robustness and reliability.
本文的研究背景强调了大型语言模型（LLM）安全对齐研究面临的挑战，特别是由于小数据集、方法不一致和不可靠的评估设置带来的噪声。过去的方法在这些问题上存在困难，导致在公平评估和比较攻击与防御时遇到障碍，从而阻碍了该领域的进展。提出的方法系统分析了LLM安全评估流程，识别了各个阶段的关键问题，并提供了减少未来评估中的噪声和偏差的指导方针。本文的贡献在于全面审查评估过程及其改善安全评估稳健性的实用建议。该方法论涉及对数据集策划、优化策略、响应生成和使用LLM评审的评估的详细分析，最终旨在提高结果的可比性并促进LLM安全研究的可测量进展。
Babel: Jailbreaking Safety Attention via Obfuscation Distribution Optimized Sampling
Authors: Ziwei Wang, Jing Chen, Ruichao Liang, Zhi Wang, Yebo Feng, Ju Jia, Ruiying Du, Cong Wu, Yang Liu
First: 2026-05-18T07:27:59+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-18T07:27:59+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Despite rigorous safety alignment, Large Language Models (LLMs) remain vulnerable to jailbreak attacks. Existing black-box methods often rely on heuristic templates or exhaustive trials, lacking mechanistic interpretability and query efficiency. In this study, we investigate an intrinsic vulnerability in the safety mechanisms of LLMs, where safety alignment relies on a small set of sparsely distributed attention heads, leaving much of the representational space weakly monitored. We formalize this phenomenon with a mathematical jailbreaking model that characterizes the delicate boundary of effective text obfuscation and analytically explains observed jailbreak behaviors. Guided by this model, we propose Babel, an efficient black-box attack framework that exploits the identified safety gap through systematic obfuscation sampling with iterative, feedback-driven distribution refinement, enabling reliable and high-success jailbreak attacks without access to model internals. Comprehensive evaluations on frontier commercial models demonstrate that Babel achieves state-of-the-art attack success rates and superior query efficiency. Specifically, compared to state-of-the-art methods, Babel increases the attack success rate on GPT-4o from 41.33% to 82.67% and on Claude-3-5-haiku from 38.33% to 78.33% within an average of 40 queries, providing a robust red-teaming methodology for LLMs safety research.
中文标题/摘要
标题：巴别：通过模糊分布优化采样破解安全注意力
尽管进行了严格的安全对齐，大型语言模型（LLMs）仍然容易受到越狱攻击。现有的黑箱方法通常依赖于启发式模板或穷举试验，缺乏机制可解释性和查询效率。在本研究中，我们调查了LLMs安全机制中的内在脆弱性，其中安全对齐依赖于一小组稀疏分布的注意力头，导致大部分表示空间监控不足。我们用数学越狱模型形式化这一现象，描述有效文本模糊化的微妙边界，并分析观察到的越狱行为。在该模型的指导下，我们提出了Babel，一个高效的黑箱攻击框架，通过系统的模糊采样和迭代反馈驱动的分布优化，利用识别出的安全漏洞，实现可靠且高成功率的越狱攻击，而无需访问模型内部。对前沿商业模型的全面评估表明，Babel实现了最先进的攻击成功率和优越的查询效率。具体而言，与最先进的方法相比，Babel将GPT-4o的攻击成功率从41.33%提高到82.67%，将Claude-3-5-haiku的攻击成功率从38.33%提高到78.33%，平均在40个查询内，提供了一种强大的红队方法论用于LLMs安全研究。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the vulnerability of Large Language Models (LLMs) to jailbreak attacks despite safety alignment efforts. Previous methods have relied on heuristic templates or exhaustive trials, which lack mechanistic interpretability and query efficiency. The proposed approach, Babel, differs by identifying a specific safety gap in LLMs' attention mechanisms and formalizing it through a mathematical jailbreaking model. This model enables systematic obfuscation sampling with iterative feedback, improving the reliability and success of jailbreak attacks without needing access to the model's internals. The contribution of this paper is the development of Babel, which achieves state-of-the-art attack success rates, increasing the success rate on GPT-4o from 41.33% to 82.67% and on Claude-3-5-haiku from 38.33% to 78.33% within an average of 40 queries, thus providing a robust methodology for LLM safety research.
本文探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）在监狱攻击中的脆弱性，指出现有的黑箱方法往往依赖于启发式模板或穷举试验，缺乏机制可解释性和查询效率。提出的方法Babel与这些方法不同，它识别了LLMs中安全对齐集中在有限数量的注意力头上的内在安全缺口，从而允许通过系统的模糊采样方法进行迭代分布优化。本文的贡献在于开发了一个数学监狱攻击模型，解释了监狱攻击行为，并指导Babel框架，该框架在攻击成功率和查询效率上达到了最先进的水平。评估结果表明，Babel显著提高了对GPT-4o和Claude-3-5-haiku等模型的攻击成功率，分别从41.33%提高到82.67%和从38.33%提高到78.33%，在平均40次查询内实现，从而为LLMs安全研究提供了强有力的方法论。
IndicSafe: A Benchmark for Evaluating Multilingual LLM Safety in South Asia
Authors: Priyaranjan Pattnayak, Sanchari Chowdhuri
First: 2026-03-18T16:54:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-15T17:06:15+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large language models (LLMs) are deployed in multilingual settings, their safety behavior in culturally diverse, low-resource languages remains poorly understood. We present the first systematic evaluation of LLM safety across 12 Indic languages, spoken by over 1.2 billion people but underrepresented in LLM training data. Using a dataset of 6,000 culturally grounded prompts spanning caste, religion, gender, health, and politics, we assess 10 leading LLMs on translated variants of the prompt. Our analysis reveals significant safety drift: cross-language agreement is just 12.8\%, and \texttt{SAFE} rate variance exceeds 17\% across languages. Some models over-refuse benign prompts in low-resource scripts, overflag politically sensitive topics, while others fail to flag unsafe generations. We quantify these failures using prompt-level entropy, category bias scores, and multilingual consistency indices. Our findings highlight critical safety generalization gaps in multilingual LLMs and show that safety alignment does not transfer evenly across languages. We release \textsc{IndicSafe}, the first benchmark to enable culturally informed safety evaluation for Indic deployments, and advocate for language-aware alignment strategies grounded in regional harms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：IndicSafe：评估南亚多语言LLM安全性的基准
随着大型语言模型（LLMs）在多语言环境中的部署，它们在文化多样性和资源匮乏语言中的安全行为仍然不够了解。我们首次系统性地评估了12种印地语言的LLM安全性，这些语言由超过12亿人使用，但在LLM训练数据中代表性不足。使用涵盖种姓、宗教、性别、健康和政治的6000个文化背景提示的数据集，我们评估了10个领先的LLM在提示翻译变体上的表现。 我们的分析揭示了显著的安全漂移：跨语言一致性仅为12.8%，而安全率方差在不同语言间超过17%。一些模型在资源匮乏的脚本中过度拒绝良性提示，过度标记政治敏感话题，而其他模型则未能标记不安全的生成。我们使用提示级熵、类别偏差分数和多语言一致性指数量化这些失败。 我们的发现突显了多语言LLM中关键的安全泛化差距，并表明安全对齐在不同语言间并不均匀转移。我们发布了IndicSafe，这是第一个基准，旨在为印地语言的文化知情安全评估提供支持，并倡导基于区域危害的语言意识对齐策略。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the urgent need to evaluate the safety of large language models (LLMs) in multilingual contexts, particularly in South Asia where 12 Indic languages are spoken by over 1.2 billion people but are underrepresented in LLM training data. Previous methods lacked systematic evaluation and often failed to account for cultural nuances, leading to significant safety issues. The proposed approach, IndicSafe, systematically assesses LLM safety using a dataset of 6,000 culturally relevant prompts, revealing a mere 12.8% cross-language agreement and over 17% variance in safety rates across languages. This research contributes by highlighting critical safety generalization gaps in multilingual LLMs and advocating for language-aware alignment strategies. The methodology involves analyzing prompt-level entropy, category bias scores, and multilingual consistency indices, demonstrating the need for improved safety measures in LLMs, which is crucial for their deployment in diverse linguistic settings.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）在多语言环境中的安全行为，特别是在文化多样性和资源匮乏的语言中，这些领域在以往研究中评估不足。以往的方法往往忽视了这些语言的独特文化背景，导致安全性漂移和不同语言之间表现不一致。所提出的方法通过使用6000个文化相关提示的数据集，系统地评估了12种印度语言的LLM安全性，揭示了安全性泛化和对齐的关键差距。该方法论包括对10种领先的LLM在翻译提示上的评估，通过提示级熵和类别偏差分数等多种指标量化失败。研究结果表明，安全性对齐在不同语言之间并不均匀转移，IndicSafe基准的引入旨在促进文化知情的安全评估，最终支持在印度语言环境中提高LLM安全性的目标。
Graph-Regularized Sparse Autoencoders for LLM Safety Steering
Authors: Jehyeok Yeon, Federico Cinus, Yifan Wu, Luca Luceri
First: 2025-12-07T04:46:30+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-15T09:56:17+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Sparse autoencoders (SAEs) are increasingly used to extract activation directions for inference-time steering, but their standard sparsity objective treats latent features as independent. This prior can be poorly matched to high-level safety behaviors, where refusal and harmful compliance appear to depend on distributed structure in activation space. We introduce Graph-Regularized Sparse Autoencoders (GSAE), a dictionary-learning method that learns safety-steering directions by smoothing SAE decoder vectors over a neuron co-activation graph and applying the resulting direction bank through a two-gate runtime controller. Empirically, GSAE improves selective refusal across JailbreakBench, HarmBench, and XSTest, increasing harmful-request refusal while keeping benign-prompt refusals low. On Llama-3-8B, replacing the standard SAE with GSAE in an otherwise identical pipeline improves $Δ_s$ by $20.1$ points on JailbreakBench and $16.8$ points on HarmBench. GSAE outperforms activation-steering baselines and black-box guardrails, preserves benign-task performance, generalizes across Llama-3, Mistral, Qwen 2.5, and Phi-4, and remains strong under black-box and gray-box jailbreak attacks.
中文标题/摘要
标题：图正则化稀疏自编码器用于大型语言模型安全引导
稀疏自编码器（SAE）越来越多地用于提取推理时引导的激活方向，但其标准稀疏性目标将潜在特征视为独立。这一先验可能与高层次的安全行为不匹配，其中拒绝和有害的顺从似乎依赖于激活空间中的分布结构。我们引入图正则化稀疏自编码器（GSAE），这是一种字典学习方法，通过在神经元共同激活图上平滑SAE解码器向量来学习安全引导方向，并通过双门运行时控制器应用结果方向库。实证结果表明，GSAE在JailbreakBench、HarmBench和XSTest上改善了选择性拒绝，增加了有害请求的拒绝，同时保持良性提示的拒绝率较低。在Llama-3-8B上，在其他条件相同的管道中用GSAE替换标准SAE，使得JailbreakBench的$Δ_s$提高了$20.1$点，HarmBench提高了$16.8$点。GSAE优于激活引导基线和黑箱护栏，保持良性任务性能，在Llama-3、Mistral、Qwen 2.5和Phi-4上具有良好的泛化能力，并在黑箱和灰箱越狱攻击下表现强劲。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of standard sparse autoencoders (SAEs) in safety steering for large language models (LLMs), where the independence assumption of latent features fails to capture the distributed nature of safety behaviors. Previous methods inadequately handle the interdependencies in activation space, leading to suboptimal performance in selective refusal tasks. The proposed Graph-Regularized Sparse Autoencoders (GSAE) enhance safety steering by incorporating a neuron co-activation graph to smooth decoder vectors, thus creating a more effective direction bank for a two-gate runtime controller. This approach is well-motivated as it directly targets the shortcomings of existing methods. The contribution of the paper lies in demonstrating that GSAE significantly improves harmful-request refusal rates while maintaining benign-prompt performance, achieving a notable increase in performance metrics on JailbreakBench and HarmBench, with improvements of 20.1 and 16.8 points respectively, and showing robustness across various LLMs and attack scenarios.
本研究解决了标准稀疏自编码器（SAE）在大型语言模型（LLM）安全引导中的局限性，因其对潜在特征的独立性假设未能捕捉安全行为的分布特性。以往的方法未能有效处理拒绝和有害合规的复杂性，导致安全任务中的表现不佳。提出的图正则化稀疏自编码器（GSAE）通过结合神经元共激活图来平滑解码器向量，从而增强安全引导方向的学习，解决了传统SAE的不足。该方法的提出是有充分动机的，因为它直接针对提高LLM安全行为的需求。实证结果表明，GSAE在JailbreakBench和HarmBench等基准测试中显著提高了选择性拒绝率，在JailbreakBench上提高了20.1个百分点，在HarmBench上提高了16.8个百分点，同时保持了对良性任务的性能，并在多种模型中具有良好的泛化能力，从而支持了增强LLM安全性的目标。
Benchmark of Benchmarks: Unpacking Influence and Code Repository Quality in LLM Safety Benchmarks
Authors: Junjie Chu, Xinyue Shen, Ye Leng, Michael Backes, Yun Shen, Yang Zhang
First: 2026-03-03T09:10:45+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T18:30:07+00:00
Comments: 24 pages. 19 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
The rapid expansion of research in LLM safety presents challenges in tracking advancements, making benchmarks important evaluation infrastructures for identifying key trends and facilitating systematic comparisons. Yet no systematic assessment exists of their code quality and runnability, nor of what factors are associated with the community's adoption of certain benchmarks over others. To address this gap, we conduct a systematic measurement study of 31 LLM safety benchmarks (covering prompt injection, jailbreak, and hallucination) with 382 non-benchmark papers as a control group, combining automated static analysis, human runnability testing (220+ person-hours), and bibliometric analysis. We find that only 39\% of benchmark repositories can run without modification, only 16\% provide flawless installation guides, and a mere 6\% include ethical considerations despite containing potentially harmful content. These deficiencies persist across the study period with no significant improvement. Analyzing adoption factors, we find that benchmark adoption correlates with author prominence and code runnability, but not with code quality standards such as Pylint score and maintainability, suggesting that the community's benchmark selection does not reward higher coding standards. Based on these results, we identify potential safety and reliability concerns. Some safety benchmark repositories openly expose harmful content, such as successful jailbreak responses, without any ethical warning or access control, effectively serving as unguarded attack resources. Furthermore, when benchmarks require ad-hoc modifications to run, downstream safety evaluations across different papers may not be comparable. We present case studies illustrating these concrete consequences and propose a targeted checklist to help benchmark contributors improve code quality, documentation, and ethical practices.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基准中的基准：解读LLM安全基准中的影响力和代码库质量
LLM安全研究的快速扩展带来了跟踪进展的挑战，使基准成为识别关键趋势和促进系统比较的重要评估基础设施。然而，目前尚无对其代码质量和可运行性的系统评估，也没有研究社区对某些基准的采用与其他基准之间的关联因素。为了解决这一空白，我们对31个LLM安全基准（涵盖提示注入、越狱和幻觉）进行系统测量研究，并以382篇非基准论文作为对照组，结合自动静态分析、人为可运行性测试（220+人小时）和文献计量分析。我们发现，只有39%的基准代码库可以在不修改的情况下运行，只有16%提供无瑕疵的安装指南，尽管包含潜在有害内容，但仅有6%考虑了伦理问题。这些缺陷在研究期间持续存在，没有显著改善。在分析采用因素时，我们发现基准采用与作者知名度和代码可运行性相关，但与代码质量标准（如Pylint评分和可维护性）无关，这表明社区的基准选择并未奖励更高的编码标准。基于这些结果，我们识别出潜在的安全和可靠性问题。一些安全基准代码库公开暴露有害内容，例如成功的越狱响应，而没有任何伦理警告或访问控制，实际上充当了无防护的攻击资源。此外，当基准需要临时修改才能运行时，不同论文之间的下游安全评估可能无法比较。我们展示了这些具体后果的案例研究，并提出了一份针对性的检查清单，以帮助基准贡献者提高代码质量、文档和伦理实践。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the challenges in evaluating LLM safety benchmarks due to the rapid growth in this field, highlighting the lack of systematic assessments of code quality and runnability. Previous methods did not adequately evaluate these aspects, leading to issues such as poor installation guides and ethical considerations in benchmark repositories. The proposed approach involves a systematic measurement study of 31 LLM safety benchmarks and a control group of 382 non-benchmark papers, utilizing automated static analysis, human runnability testing, and bibliometric analysis. The findings reveal significant deficiencies in benchmark repositories, with only 39% runnable without modification and a concerning lack of ethical considerations. This study contributes to identifying safety and reliability concerns in benchmark adoption and proposes a checklist for improving code quality and ethical practices in future benchmarks.
本研究解决了由于大型语言模型（LLM）相关基准的快速增长而导致的安全评估挑战，这些基准缺乏对代码质量和可运行性的系统评估。以往的方法未能充分评估这些基准，导致可运行性低和文档不完善等问题。本研究系统地测量了31个LLM安全基准，并与382篇非基准论文进行了比较，采用了自动分析、人为测试和文献计量分析。研究结果显示，许多基准库在没有修改的情况下无法运行，安装指南不足，缺乏伦理考虑，提出了安全隐患。本文的贡献在于识别这些缺陷并提出改进基准质量和伦理实践的检查表，从而增强研究中安全评估的可比性。
The Great Pretender: A Stochasticity Problem in LLM Jailbreak
Authors: Jean-Philippe Monteuuis, Cong Chen, Jonathan Petit
First: 2026-05-14T06:05:37+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T06:05:37+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
"Oh-Oh, yes, I'm the great pretender. Pretending that I'm doing well. My need is such, I pretend too much..." summarizes the state in the area of jailbreak creation and evaluation. You find this method to generate adversarial attacks proposed by a reputable institution (e.g., BoN from Anthropic or Crescendo from Microsoft Research). However, this method does not deliver on the promise claimed in the paper despite having top ASR scores against industry-grade LLMs. You successfully generate the jailbreak prompts against your target (open) model. However, the generated jailbreak prompt works against the target model with a 50% consecutive success rate (5 out of 10 attempts) despite having an 80% ASR (on paper) on the latest closed-source model (with a guardrail system)! This observation leads us to think. First, Attack Success Rate (ASR), the primary metric for LLM jailbreak benchmarking, is not a stable quantity. Second, published ASR numbers are therefore systematically inflated and incomparable across papers. Therefore, we wonder "Why a successful jailbreak prompt does not perform consistently well against a target model on which the prompts have been optimized?". To answer this question, we study the impact of stochasticity not only during attack evaluation but also during attack generation. Our evaluation includes several jailbreak attacks, models (different sizes and providers), and judges. In addition, we propose a new metric and two new frameworks (CAS-eval and CAS-gen). Our evaluation framework, CAS-eval, shows that an attack can have an ASR drop of up to 30 percentage points when a jailbreak prompt needs to succeed on more than one attempt. Thankfully, our attack generation framework (CAS-gen) improves previous jailbreak methods and helps them recover this loss of 30 percentage points!
中文标题/摘要
标题：伟大的伪装者：LLM越狱中的随机性问题
"哦-哦，是的，我是伟大的伪装者。假装我很好。我的需求如此，我假装得太多……"总结了越狱创建和评估领域的现状。你发现了由一个知名机构（例如，Anthropic的BoN或微软研究院的Crescendo）提出的生成对抗攻击的方法。然而，尽管在行业级LLM上具有顶级的攻击成功率（ASR），该方法并未兑现论文中所声称的承诺。你成功生成了针对目标（开放）模型的越狱提示。然而，生成的越狱提示在目标模型上的连续成功率为50%（10次尝试中有5次成功），尽管在最新的闭源模型（带有护栏系统）上在纸面上有80%的ASR！这一观察促使我们思考。首先，攻击成功率（ASR），作为LLM越狱基准测试的主要指标，并不是一个稳定的量。其次，发布的ASR数字因此系统性地被夸大，并且在不同论文之间不可比。因此，我们想知道“为什么成功的越狱提示在经过优化的目标模型上表现不一致？”为了回答这个问题，我们研究了随机性在攻击评估和攻击生成过程中的影响。我们的评估包括几种越狱攻击、模型（不同大小和提供者）和评审。此外，我们提出了一种新指标和两个新框架（CAS-eval和CAS-gen）。我们的评估框架CAS-eval显示，当越狱提示需要在多次尝试中成功时，攻击的ASR可能下降多达30个百分点。值得庆幸的是，我们的攻击生成框架（CAS-gen）改进了之前的越狱方法，并帮助它们恢复这30个百分点的损失！
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the inconsistencies in the effectiveness of jailbreak prompts for large language models (LLMs), highlighting that existing methods, despite high Attack Success Rates (ASR), often fail to deliver reliable results in practical applications. Previous approaches have shown inflated ASR metrics that do not account for stochasticity during both attack generation and evaluation, leading to misleading conclusions about their effectiveness. This paper contributes by proposing a new evaluation framework (CAS-eval) and an attack generation framework (CAS-gen) that account for these stochastic factors, demonstrating that ASR can drop significantly when prompts are tested across multiple attempts. The methodology includes a comprehensive evaluation of various jailbreak attacks and models, revealing that the proposed frameworks can recover up to 30 percentage points in ASR loss, thereby enhancing the reliability of jailbreak prompts in real-world scenarios.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLMs）越狱提示的有效性不一致性，强调现有方法（如来自知名机构的方法）通常报告的攻击成功率（ASR）被夸大，无法反映实际性能。所提出的方法通过引入对越狱提示生成和评估中随机性的关注，与以往方法有所不同。该研究的贡献在于开发了两个新框架，CAS-eval和CAS-gen，提供了对越狱有效性更准确的评估，并提高了攻击生成的可靠性。通过对各种模型和攻击的全面评估，研究表明，CAS-eval框架揭示了在多次测试提示时ASR显著下降，而CAS-gen有效缓解了这一损失，实现了越狱尝试中更稳定的性能。
Reducing the Safety Tax in LLM Safety Alignment with On-Policy Self-Distillation
Authors: Yu Fu, Longxuan Yu, Haz Sameen Shahgir, Zhipeng Wei, Hui Liu, N. Benjamin Erichson, Yue Dong
First: 2026-05-14T03:40:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-14T03:40:07+00:00
Comments: 20 pages, 5 figures
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Safety alignment often improves robustness to harmful queries at the cost of reasoning ability, a tradeoff known as the safety tax. A common cause is distributional mismatch: supervised fine-tuning trains the target model on safety demonstrations produced by humans, external models, or fixed self-generated traces, rather than on trajectories sampled from its own policy. We identify off-policy training mismatch as a second source of this tax and study on-policy self-distillation for safety alignment, which we call OPSA. The model generates its own rollouts and receives dense per-token KL supervision from a frozen teacher copy of itself conditioned on a privileged safety context. Because this teacher must be safer than the sampled student trajectory, we introduce \emph{teacher flip rate}: a criterion that measures how often a privileged context converts unsafe responses into safe ones. We use this signal to search for contexts that activate latent safety reasoning rather than merely elicit safe-looking demonstrations. Across two reasoning-model families and five model scales, OPSA achieves a stronger safety--reasoning tradeoff than off-policy self-distillation and external-teacher distillation under matched data and full-parameter fine-tuning, with the largest gains on smaller models (+8.85 points on R1-Distill-1.5B and +5.49 points on Qwen3-0.6B). The gains persist across training-set sizes and adaptive jailbreak evaluations. Token-level analyses further show that OPSA concentrates updates near early compliance-decision tokens, providing a mechanism for improving safety while preserving general reasoning.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过策略自蒸馏减少大型语言模型安全对齐中的安全税
安全对齐通常在提高对有害查询的鲁棒性的同时牺牲推理能力，这种权衡被称为安全税。一个常见原因是分布不匹配：监督微调在由人类、外部模型或固定自生成轨迹产生的安全示例上训练目标模型，而不是在其自身策略采样的轨迹上。我们将离策略训练不匹配识别为这种税的第二个来源，并研究用于安全对齐的策略自蒸馏，称为OPSA。该模型生成自己的回滚，并从一个冻结的教师副本中接收每个标记的密集KL监督，该副本基于特权安全上下文进行条件化。由于这个教师必须比采样的学生轨迹更安全，我们引入了“教师翻转率”：一个衡量特权上下文将不安全响应转化为安全响应的频率的标准。我们利用这个信号寻找激活潜在安全推理的上下文，而不仅仅是引出看似安全的示例。在两个推理模型系列和五个模型规模中，OPSA在匹配数据和全参数微调下实现了比离策略自蒸馏和外部教师蒸馏更强的安全-推理权衡，在较小模型上获得了最大的提升（R1-Distill-1.5B上提高8.85分，Qwen3-0.6B上提高5.49分）。这些提升在训练集大小和自适应越狱评估中持续存在。标记级分析进一步表明，OPSA将更新集中在早期合规决策标记附近，提供了一种在保持一般推理的同时提高安全性的机制。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the challenge of safety alignment in large language models (LLMs), where enhancing robustness to harmful queries often compromises reasoning ability, a phenomenon termed the safety tax. Previous methods, including off-policy self-distillation and external-teacher distillation, suffer from distributional mismatch and fail to leverage the model's own policy for training, leading to suboptimal safety-reasoning tradeoffs. The proposed approach, on-policy self-distillation for safety alignment (OPSA), mitigates these issues by allowing the model to generate its own rollouts and receive supervision from a safer teacher model, thus improving the safety-reasoning balance. The paper contributes by demonstrating that OPSA achieves significant performance improvements, particularly in smaller models, with gains of +8.85 points on R1-Distill-1.5B and +5.49 points on Qwen3-0.6B, while maintaining safety across various training conditions and evaluations. The methodology emphasizes token-level updates that enhance compliance decisions, effectively addressing the safety tax while preserving reasoning capabilities.
本文探讨了大型语言模型（LLMs）中的安全对齐挑战，这通常导致所谓的安全税权衡，即提高对有害查询的鲁棒性会损害推理能力。以往的方法，包括离线训练和外部教师蒸馏，存在分布不匹配的问题，未能有效利用模型自身策略进行安全演示。所提出的方法，即用于安全对齐的在线自蒸馏（OPSA），通过允许模型生成自己的回滚并从冻结的教师模型中接收监督，减轻了这些问题，从而在不牺牲性能的情况下增强安全推理。该研究的贡献在于证明OPSA在安全与推理的权衡上优于现有方法，在较小模型上观察到显著的性能提升，R1-Distill-1.5B上提高了8.85分，Qwen3-0.6B上提高了5.49分，同时在各种训练条件和评估中保持了鲁棒性。
Quantifying LLM Safety Degradation Under Repeated Attacks Using Survival Analysis
Authors: Zvi Topol
First: 2026-05-13T01:26:06+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-13T01:26:06+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) are increasingly deployed in a wide range of applications, yet remain vulnerable to adversarial jailbreak attacks that circumvent their safety guardrails. Existing evaluation frameworks typically report binary success/failure metrics, failing to capture the temporal dynamics of how attacks succeed under persistent adversarial pressure. This preliminary work proposes a novel evaluation framework that applies survival analysis techniques to characterize LLM jailbreak vuln`erability. Our approach models the time-to-jailbreak as a survival outcome, enabling estimation of hazard functions, survival curves, and risk factors associated with successful attacks. We evaluate three LLMs against a subset of prompts from the HarmBench dataset spanning three attack categories. Our analysis reveals that models exhibit distinct vulnerability profiles: while one model demonstrates rapid degradation under iterative attacks, the two other models show consistent moderate vulnerability. Our framework provides actionable insights for model and LLM application developers and establishes survival analysis as a rigorous methodology for LLM safety evaluation.
中文标题/摘要
标题：使用生存分析量化在重复攻击下的大型语言模型安全性退化
大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地应用于各种场景，但仍然容易受到绕过安全防护的对抗性越狱攻击。现有评估框架通常报告二元成功/失败指标，未能捕捉在持续对抗压力下攻击成功的时间动态。本初步工作提出了一种新颖的评估框架，应用生存分析技术来表征LLM越狱脆弱性。我们的方法将越狱时间建模为生存结果，使得能够估计危险函数、生存曲线和与成功攻击相关的风险因素。我们对三个LLM进行了评估，使用来自HarmBench数据集的子集提示，涵盖三种攻击类别。我们的分析揭示模型表现出不同的脆弱性特征：虽然一个模型在迭代攻击下迅速退化，但另外两个模型则表现出一致的中等脆弱性。我们的框架为模型和LLM应用开发者提供了可操作的见解，并确立了生存分析作为LLM安全评估的严格方法论。

The research addresses the vulnerability of large language models (LLMs) to adversarial jailbreak attacks, which undermine their safety features. Previous evaluation methods primarily relied on binary success or failure metrics, which inadequately captured the dynamics of attack success over time. The proposed approach utilizes survival analysis to assess LLM vulnerability by modeling the time-to-jailbreak as a survival outcome, thus allowing for the estimation of hazard functions and survival curves. This methodology is well-motivated as it provides a more nuanced understanding of model vulnerabilities under repeated attacks. The study evaluates three LLMs using prompts from the HarmBench dataset and finds that while one model shows rapid degradation under iterative attacks, the other two maintain moderate vulnerability, offering valuable insights for developers in enhancing LLM safety evaluation.

RACC: Representation-Aware Coverage Criteria for LLM Safety Testing
Authors: Zeming Wei, Zhixin Zhang, Chengcan Wu, Yihao Zhang, Xiaokun Luan, Meng Sun
First: 2026-02-02T16:20:51+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-12T03:47:11+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large Language Models (LLMs) face severe safety risks from jailbreak attacks, yet current safety testing largely relies on static datasets and lacks systematic criteria to evaluate test suite quality and adequacy. While coverage criteria have proven effective for smaller neural networks, they are impractical for LLMs due to computational overhead and the entanglement of safety-critical signals with irrelevant neuron activations. To address these issues, we propose RACC (Representation-Aware Coverage Criteria), a set of coverage criteria specialized for LLM safety testing. RACC first extracts safety representations from the LLM's hidden states using a small calibration set of harmful prompts, then measures test prompts' concept activations against these directions, and finally computes coverage through six criteria assessing both individual and compositional safety concept coverage. Experiments on multiple LLMs and safety benchmarks show that RACC reliably rewards high-quality jailbreak test suites while remaining insensitive to redundant or invalid inputs, which is a key distinction that neuron-level criteria fail to make. We further demonstrate RACC's practical value in two applications, including test suite prioritization and attack prompt sampling, and validate its generalization across diverse settings and configurations. Overall, RACC provides a scalable and principled foundation for coverage-guided LLM safety testing.
中文标题/摘要
标题：RACC：面向表示的LLM安全测试覆盖标准
大型语言模型（LLM）面临来自越狱攻击的严重安全风险，但当前的安全测试主要依赖静态数据集，缺乏系统性标准来评估测试套件的质量和充分性。虽然覆盖标准在较小的神经网络中已被证明有效，但由于计算开销和安全关键信号与无关神经元激活的纠缠，它们在LLM中不切实际。为了解决这些问题，我们提出了RACC（面向表示的覆盖标准），这是一组专门针对LLM安全测试的覆盖标准。RACC首先使用一小组有害提示从LLM的隐藏状态中提取安全表示，然后根据这些方向测量测试提示的概念激活，最后通过六个标准计算覆盖，评估个体和组合安全概念的覆盖。对多个LLM和安全基准的实验表明，RACC可靠地奖励高质量的越狱测试套件，同时对冗余或无效输入保持不敏感，这是神经元级标准无法做到的关键区别。我们进一步展示了RACC在两个应用中的实际价值，包括测试套件优先级排序和攻击提示采样，并验证了其在不同设置和配置中的泛化能力。总体而言，RACC为覆盖引导的LLM安全测试提供了可扩展和原则性的基础。

The research addresses the significant safety risks posed by jailbreak attacks on Large Language Models (LLMs), highlighting the inadequacies of current safety testing methods that rely on static datasets and lack systematic criteria for evaluating test suite quality. Previous methods, while effective for smaller neural networks, are impractical for LLMs due to high computational demands and the mixing of safety signals with irrelevant neuron activations. The proposed approach, RACC (Representation-Aware Coverage Criteria), overcomes these limitations by extracting safety representations from LLM hidden states using a small calibration set and measuring test prompts' concept activations against these representations, thus providing a more nuanced assessment of coverage. The paper contributes a scalable framework for LLM safety testing, demonstrating that RACC effectively prioritizes high-quality jailbreak test suites and remains robust against irrelevant inputs, achieving reliable performance across multiple LLMs and safety benchmarks, which supports its intended goals.

FragBench: Cross-Session Attacks Hidden in Benign-Looking Fragments
Authors: Astha Mehta, Niruthiha Selvanayagam, Cedric Lam, Hengxu Li, Phuc-Nguyen Nguyen, Raymond Lee, Olivia McGoffin, My, Luong, Arthur Collé, Jamie Johnson, David Williams-King, Linh Le
First: 2026-05-10T21:06:48+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-10T21:06:48+00:00
Comments: preprint of submission
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
An attacker can split a malicious goal into sub-prompts that each look benign on their own and only become harmful in combination. Existing LLM safety benchmarks evaluate prompts one at a time, or across turns of a single chat, and so do not look for a malicious signal spread across separate sessions with no shared context. We build FragBench, a benchmark drawn from 24 real-world cyber-incident campaigns, which keeps the full attack trail: the multi-fragment kill chain, the per-fragment safety-judge verdicts, sandboxed execution traces, and a matched set of benign cover sessions. FragBench splits this trail into two paired tasks: an adversarial rewriter that hardens fragments against a single-turn safety judge (FragBench Attack), and a graph-based user-level detector trained on the resulting interactions (FragBench Defense). The single-turn judge is near chance on the released corpus by construction, but four GNN variants and three classical-ML baselines all recover the cross-session feature, reaching aggregate event-level F1 = 0.88-0.96. Defending against fragmented LLM misuse therefore requires modeling the cross-session interaction graph, rather than isolated prompts. Our generator, rewriter, sandbox harness, and detector are released at https://github.com/LidaSafety/fragbench.
中文标题/摘要
标题：FragBench：隐藏在看似良性片段中的跨会话攻击
攻击者可以将恶意目标拆分为看似良性的子提示，这些子提示单独看时无害，但组合在一起时会变得有害。现有的LLM安全基准一次评估一个提示，或在单个聊天的多个回合中评估，因此未能寻找跨会话的恶意信号，这些会话之间没有共享上下文。我们构建了FragBench，这是一个基于24个真实网络事件活动的基准，保留了完整的攻击轨迹：多片段杀伤链、每个片段的安全评判结果、沙箱执行痕迹，以及一组匹配的良性覆盖会话。FragBench将这一轨迹分为两个配对任务：一个对抗重写器，旨在增强片段对单回合安全评判的抵抗力（FragBench Attack），以及一个基于图的用户级检测器，训练于结果交互（FragBench Defense）。单回合评判在发布的语料库中几乎是随机的，但四种GNN变体和三种经典机器学习基线都恢复了跨会话特征，达到聚合事件级F1 = 0.88-0.96。因此，防御碎片化的LLM误用需要建模跨会话交互图，而不是孤立的提示。我们的生成器、重写器、沙箱工具和检测器已发布在https://github.com/LidaSafety/fragbench。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the challenge of detecting cross-session attacks in large language models (LLMs), where malicious prompts are split into benign-looking fragments that only become harmful when combined. Previous methods evaluated prompts in isolation or within a single chat session, failing to capture the malicious signals that can emerge across different sessions without shared context. The proposed approach, FragBench, introduces a benchmark that retains the complete attack trail from real-world cyber incidents and divides it into two tasks: an adversarial rewriter to strengthen fragments against single-turn safety judges and a graph-based user-level detector trained on these interactions. The methodology demonstrates that effective defense against fragmented LLM misuse requires understanding cross-session interactions, achieving an aggregate event-level F1 score between 0.88 and 0.96, thus supporting the goal of enhancing LLM safety against sophisticated attacks.
本研究解决了在大型语言模型（LLM）中检测跨会话攻击的挑战，其中恶意提示可以在不同会话中伪装成良性片段。以往的方法评估提示时往往孤立或仅限于单一聊天会话，未能识别跨多个交互且没有共享上下文的威胁。所提出的FragBench基准通过分析来自真实网络事件的综合数据集，克服了这些局限性，允许通过双任务方法评估碎片化攻击：对抗重写器和基于图的用户级检测器。该方法论表明，有效防御碎片化LLM滥用需要理解会话之间的交互，使用多种模型实现了0.88到0.96之间的事件级F1得分。这一表现表明，所提出的方法非常适合其增强LLM安全性以应对复杂攻击策略的目标。
Theoretical Limits of Language Model Alignment
Authors: Lucas Monteiro Paes, Natalie Mackraz, Barry-John Theobald, Federico Danieli
First: 2026-05-08T01:32:22+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-08T01:32:22+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Language model (LM) alignment improves model outputs to reflect human preferences while preserving the capabilities of the base model. The most common alignment approaches are (i) reinforcement learning, which maximizes the expected reward under a KL-divergence constraint, and (ii) best-of-$N$ alignment, which selects the highest-reward output among $N$ independent samples. Despite their widespread use, the fundamental limits of reward improvement under a KL budget remain poorly understood. We characterize the information-theoretic limits of KL-regularized alignment by deriving the maximum achievable expected reward gain for a fixed KL-divergence budget. Our first result provides a closed-form expression for the optimal reward improvement, governed by a Jeffreys divergence term rather than the $\sqrt{\texttt{KL}}$ used in prior analyses. We further reformulate this expression as a covariance under the base model, yielding a practical estimator that predicts achievable alignment gains from base model samples alone. We extend our analysis to the proxy reward setting, showing that the gap between ideal and proxy alignment (reward hacking) grows with the magnitude of reward error and when the KL penalty factor decreases. We then prove that reward ensembling mitigates reward hacking, providing a theoretical justification for this technique used in practice. Empirically, we compute the KL-reward Pareto frontier for two tasks for LMs, safety and summarization, and show that best-of-$N$ closely approaches the theoretical limit, while PPO and GRPO remain substantially suboptimal. Our theoretical results shed light on several empirically observed phenomena in the alignment literature and suggest that algorithmic improvements are needed to achieve optimal alignment without high inference costs.
中文标题/摘要
标题：语言模型对齐的理论极限
语言模型（LM）对齐改善模型输出，使其反映人类偏好，同时保留基础模型的能力。最常见的对齐方法有（i）强化学习，在KL散度约束下最大化期望奖励，以及（ii）最佳$N$对齐，从$N$个独立样本中选择最高奖励输出。尽管这些方法被广泛使用，但在KL预算下奖励改善的基本极限仍然不甚了解。我们通过推导固定KL散度预算下可实现的最大期望奖励增益，来表征KL正则化对齐的信息论极限。我们的第一个结果提供了最优奖励改善的封闭形式表达式，该表达式由Jeffreys散度项主导，而不是先前分析中使用的$\sqrt{\texttt{KL}}$。我们进一步将该表达式重新表述为基础模型下的协方差，得出一个实用的估计器，仅通过基础模型样本预测可实现的对齐增益。我们将分析扩展到代理奖励设置，表明理想对齐与代理对齐（奖励黑客）之间的差距随着奖励误差的大小和KL惩罚因子的降低而增加。然后我们证明奖励集成可以减轻奖励黑客，为这一实践中使用的技术提供理论依据。通过实证，我们计算了两个任务（安全性和摘要）的KL-奖励帕累托前沿，并显示最佳$N$接近理论极限，而PPO和GRPO仍然显著次优。我们的理论结果阐明了对齐文献中观察到的若干经验现象，并建议需要算法改进以在不高推理成本的情况下实现最优对齐。
Summary / 总结
The research investigates the theoretical limits of language model alignment, which aims to enhance model outputs to better reflect human preferences while maintaining the model's capabilities. Previous methods, such as reinforcement learning and best-of-$N$ alignment, have not fully understood the fundamental limits of reward improvement under a KL-divergence constraint, leading to suboptimal performance. This paper proposes a new approach that derives a closed-form expression for optimal reward improvement governed by Jeffreys divergence, rather than the previously used $\sqrt{\texttt{KL}}$. The methodology includes a practical estimator for predicting alignment gains and extends the analysis to proxy rewards, demonstrating that reward ensembling can mitigate issues like reward hacking. The empirical results show that best-of-$N$ alignment closely approaches the theoretical limits for tasks like safety and summarization, while traditional methods like PPO and GRPO are significantly less effective, indicating the need for algorithmic improvements to achieve optimal alignment efficiently.
本文探讨了现有语言模型（LM）对齐方法的局限性，特别是强化学习和最佳-$N$对齐，这些方法未能充分理解在KL散度约束下奖励改进的基本限制。提出的方法通过推导最佳奖励改进的闭式表达式来表征KL正则化对齐的信息论极限，该表达式由Jeffreys散度项主导，而不是之前使用的$\sqrt{\texttt{KL}}$。这种重构导致了一个实用的估计器，可以仅基于基础模型样本预测可实现的对齐增益。论文还表明，奖励集成可以减轻奖励黑客行为，为这一技术提供了理论支持。实证结果表明，在安全性和摘要等任务中，最佳-$N$对齐接近理论极限，而传统方法如PPO和GRPO则显著次优，这表明需要算法改进以高效实现最佳对齐。
When No Benchmark Exists: Validating Comparative LLM Safety Scoring Without Ground-Truth Labels
Authors: Sushant Gautam, Finn Schwall, Annika Willoch Olstad, Fernando Vallecillos Ruiz, Birk Torpmann-Hagen, Sunniva Maria Stordal Bjørklund, Leon Moonen, Klas Pettersen, Michael A. Riegler
First: 2026-05-07T17:56:41+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T17:56:41+00:00
Comments: SimpleAudit Repository: https://github.com/kelkalot/simpleaudit
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2 · Code3
Abstract
Many deployments must compare candidate language models for safety before a labeled benchmark exists for the relevant language, sector, or regulatory regime. We formalize this setting as benchmarkless comparative safety scoring and specify the contract under which a scenario-based audit can be interpreted as deployment evidence. Scores are valid only under a fixed scenario pack, rubric, auditor, judge, sampling configuration, and rerun budget. Because no labels are available, we replace ground-truth agreement with an instrumental-validity chain: responsiveness to a controlled safe-versus-abliterated contrast, dominance of target-driven variance over auditor and judge artifacts, and stability across reruns. We instantiate the chain in SimpleAudit, a local-first scoring instrument, and validate it on a Norwegian safety pack. Safe and abliterated targets separate with AUROC values between 0.89 and 1.00, target identity is the dominant variance component ($η^2 \approx 0.52$), and severity profiles stabilize by ten reruns. Applying the same chain to Petri shows that it admits both tools. The substantial differences arise upstream of the chain, in claim-contract enforcement and deployment fit. A Norwegian public-sector procurement case comparing Borealis and Gemma 3 demonstrates the resulting evidence in practice: the safer model depends on scenario category and risk measure. Consequently, scores, matched deltas, critical rates, uncertainty, and the auditor and judge used must be reported together rather than collapsed into a single ranking.
中文标题/摘要
标题：当没有基准时：在没有真实标签的情况下验证比较LLM安全评分
许多部署必须在相关语言、行业或监管制度的标记基准存在之前比较候选语言模型的安全性。我们将这种情况形式化为无基准的比较安全评分，并指定场景基础审计可以被解释为部署证据的合同。分数仅在固定的场景包、评分标准、审计员、评判者、抽样配置和重跑预算下有效。由于没有可用的标签，我们用一个工具有效性链替代真实一致性：对受控的安全与消除对比的响应、目标驱动方差对审计员和评判者伪影的主导性，以及重跑的稳定性。我们在SimpleAudit中实例化该链，这是一个本地优先的评分工具，并在挪威安全包上验证。安全和消除目标的AUROC值在0.89到1.00之间，目标身份是主导方差成分（$η^2 \approx 0.52$），严重性轮廓在十次重跑中稳定。将相同的链应用于Petri表明它同时接受这两种工具。显著差异出现在链的上游，在索赔合同执行和部署适配中。一个比较Borealis和Gemma 3的挪威公共部门采购案例展示了实践中的证据：更安全的模型依赖于场景类别和风险度量。因此，分数、匹配的增量、关键率、不确定性以及使用的审计员和评判者必须一起报告，而不是合并为单一排名。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the challenge of evaluating the safety of language models in scenarios where no labeled benchmarks exist, which is crucial for deployments across various sectors and regulatory environments. Previous methods relied on ground-truth labels for safety assessments, which are often unavailable, leading to potential inaccuracies in model comparisons. The proposed approach, termed benchmarkless comparative safety scoring, introduces an instrumental-validity chain that emphasizes responsiveness to controlled contrasts and the dominance of target-driven variance, thereby providing a more reliable evaluation framework. The paper contributes by formalizing this new scoring method and implementing it in SimpleAudit, validated against a Norwegian safety pack, achieving AUROC values between 0.89 and 1.00, indicating strong separation between safe and abliterated targets. This methodology supports the goal of providing a robust safety evaluation process, demonstrating that the safer model can vary based on scenario categories and risk measures, necessitating comprehensive reporting of scores and associated metrics.
本研究解决了在没有标记基准的情况下评估语言模型安全性的问题，这对于确保在各个领域的安全部署至关重要。传统方法依赖于真实标签进行安全评估，而在缺乏基准的情况下，这可能会带来问题。所提出的方法称为无基准比较安全评分，提出了一种利用基于场景的审计和工具有效性链来验证安全评分的框架，而无需真实标签。该方法在名为SimpleAudit的工具中实施，并使用挪威安全包进行了验证，AUROC值在0.89到1.00之间，表明安全目标和消融目标之间的强分离。研究结果表明，所提出的方法有效捕捉基于场景类别和风险度量的安全差异，为现有评估方法提供了一个强有力的替代方案。
Beyond Accuracy: Policy Invariance as a Reliability Test for LLM Safety Judges
Authors: Shihao Weng, Yang Feng, Xiaofei Xie
First: 2026-05-07T12:49:09+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T12:49:09+00:00
Comments: 9 pages
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
LLM-as-a-Judge pipelines have become the de facto evaluator for agent safety, yet existing benchmarks treat their verdicts as ground-truth proxies without checking whether the verdicts depend on the agent's behavior or merely on how the evaluation policy happens to be worded. We argue that any trustworthy safety judge must satisfy a basic property we call policy invariance, and we operationalize it as three testable principles: rubric-semantics invariance under certified-equivalent rewrites, rubric-threshold invariance under intentional strict-to-lenient shifts, and ambiguity-aware calibration so that verdict instability concentrates on genuinely ambiguous cases. Instantiating these principles as a stress-test protocol with four agent-class judges on trajectories drawn from ASSEBench and R-Judge, we surface a previously unmeasured failure mode: today's judges respond to meaningful normative shifts and to meaningless structural rewrites with comparable strength, and cannot tell the two apart. Content-preserving policy rewrites flip up to 9.1% of verdicts above baseline jitter, and 18-43% of all observed flips occur on unambiguous cases under such rewrites, so existing safety scores conflate what the agent did with how the evaluator was prompted. Beyond the diagnosis, we contribute the Policy Invariance Score and the Judge Card reporting protocol, which expose an order-of-magnitude spread in judge reliability that is invisible to accuracy-only leaderboards. We release the protocol and code so that future agent-safety benchmarks can audit their own evaluators rather than trust them by default.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越准确性：政策不变性作为LLM安全评判的可靠性测试
LLM作为评判的管道已成为代理安全的事实评估者，但现有基准将其裁决视为真实代理，而未检查裁决是否依赖于代理的行为或仅仅依赖于评估政策的措辞。我们认为，任何值得信赖的安全评判必须满足我们称之为政策不变性的基本属性，并将其操作化为三个可测试的原则：在经过认证的等效重写下的评分语义不变性、在有意的严格到宽松的转变下的评分阈值不变性，以及意识到歧义的校准，以便裁决的不稳定性集中在真正模糊的案例上。通过在从ASSEBench和R-Judge提取的轨迹上对四个代理类别的评判进行压力测试协议的实例化，我们揭示了一种以前未测量的失败模式：今天的评判对有意义的规范性变化和无意义的结构重写的反应强度相当，无法区分二者。内容保留的政策重写使得高达9.1%的裁决在基线抖动之上发生变化，18-43%的所有观察到的变化发生在此类重写下的明确案例中，因此现有的安全评分混淆了代理的行为与评估者的提示方式。除了诊断，我们贡献了政策不变性评分和评判卡报告协议，揭示了评判可靠性在仅依赖准确性的排行榜上不可见的数量级差异。我们发布了该协议和代码，以便未来的代理安全基准可以审计自己的评估者，而不是默认信任他们。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of current LLM-as-a-Judge systems, which often treat verdicts as reliable ground-truth proxies without verifying their dependence on agent behavior versus evaluation policy wording. Previous methods lack a rigorous examination of policy invariance, leading to potential misinterpretations of safety judgments. This paper proposes a novel approach based on three testable principles of policy invariance, operationalized through a stress-test protocol involving four agent-class judges and trajectories from ASSEBench and R-Judge. The findings reveal that existing judges cannot distinguish between meaningful normative shifts and meaningless structural rewrites, resulting in significant verdict instability, particularly in unambiguous cases. The paper contributes the Policy Invariance Score and the Judge Card reporting protocol, highlighting discrepancies in judge reliability that are not captured by traditional accuracy metrics, thus providing a framework for future evaluations of agent safety.
本研究关注用于评估代理安全性的LLM作为评判者的管道的可靠性，强调现有基准往往将评判者的裁决视为准确，而未验证其是否依赖于评估政策而非代理的行为。以往的方法缺乏系统性评估这种可靠性，可能导致对安全评分的误解。所提出的方法引入了政策不变性的概念，通过三个可测试的原则进行操作，使评估者对各种提示的反应得到更稳健的评估。这种方法揭示了一种显著的失败模式，即评判者无法区分有意义的规范性变化和微不足道的结构变化，导致误导性的裁决。本文贡献了政策不变性评分和评判者卡报告协议，提供了对评判者可靠性的更清晰理解，超越了单纯的准确性指标，证明所提出的方法有效识别了安全评估中评判者表现的差异。
XL-SafetyBench: A Country-Grounded Cross-Cultural Benchmark for LLM Safety and Cultural Sensitivity
Authors: Dasol Choi, Eugenia Kim, Jaewon Noh, Sang Seo, Eunmi Kim, Myunggyo Oh, Yunjin Park, Brigitta Jesica Kartono, Josef Pichlmeier, Helena Berndt, Sai Krishna Mendu, Glenn Johannes Tungka, Özlem Gökçe, Suresh Gehlot, Katherine Pratt, Amanda Minnich, Haon Park
First: 2026-05-07T04:35:03+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-07T04:35:03+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Current LLM safety benchmarks are predominantly English-centric and often rely on translation, failing to capture country-specific harms. Moreover, they rarely evaluate a model's ability to detect culturally embedded sensitivities as distinct from universal harms. We introduce XL-SafetyBench. a suite of 5,500 test cases across 10 country-language pairs, comprising a Jailbreak Benchmark of country-grounded adversarial prompts and a Cultural Benchmark where local sensitivities are embedded within innocuous requests. Each item is constructed via a multi-stage pipeline that combines LLM-assisted discovery, automated validation gates, and dual independent native-speaker annotators per country. To distinguish principled refusal from comprehension failure, we evaluate Attack Success Rate (ASR) alongside two complementary metrics we introduce: Neutral-Safe Rate (NSR) and Cultural Sensitivity Rate (CSR). Evaluating 10 frontier and 27 local LLMs reveals two key findings. First, jailbreak robustness and cultural awareness do not show a coupled relationship among frontier models, so a composite safety score obscures per-axis variation. Second, local models exhibit a near-linear ASR-NSR trade-off (r = -0.81), indicating that their apparent safety reflects generation failure rather than genuine alignment. XL-SafetyBench enables more nuanced, cross-cultural safety evaluation in the multilingual era.
中文标题/摘要
标题：XL-SafetyBench：一个基于国家的跨文化大型语言模型安全与文化敏感性基准
当前的大型语言模型安全基准主要以英语为中心，通常依赖翻译，未能捕捉特定国家的危害。此外，它们很少评估模型检测文化嵌入敏感性与普遍危害的能力。我们推出了XL-SafetyBench，一个包含5500个测试案例的套件，涵盖10个国家-语言对，包括一个基于国家的对抗性提示的越狱基准和一个将地方敏感性嵌入无害请求中的文化基准。每个项目通过一个多阶段流程构建，该流程结合了大型语言模型辅助发现、自动验证门和每个国家的双独立母语者注释。为了区分原则性拒绝与理解失败，我们评估攻击成功率（ASR）以及我们引入的两个互补指标：中性安全率（NSR）和文化敏感性率（CSR）。对10个前沿和27个地方大型语言模型的评估揭示了两个关键发现。首先，越狱鲁棒性与文化意识在前沿模型中并不呈现耦合关系，因此复合安全评分掩盖了每个轴的变化。其次，地方模型表现出近线性的ASR-NSR权衡（r = -0.81），表明它们的表面安全反映的是生成失败而非真正的对齐。XL-SafetyBench使得在多语言时代进行更细致的跨文化安全评估成为可能。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the limitations of existing large language model (LLM) safety benchmarks, which are primarily focused on English and often fail to account for country-specific harms and culturally embedded sensitivities. Previous methods relied heavily on translation and did not adequately evaluate the nuanced understanding of cultural contexts, leading to a lack of comprehensive safety assessments. The proposed XL-SafetyBench introduces a benchmark suite of 5,500 test cases across 10 country-language pairs, utilizing a multi-stage pipeline for item construction that includes LLM-assisted discovery and validation by native speakers. This approach allows for a more detailed evaluation of LLMs' safety and cultural sensitivity. The findings indicate that there is no consistent relationship between jailbreak robustness and cultural awareness in frontier models, and local models demonstrate a significant trade-off between attack success and safety metrics, suggesting that their safety may stem from generation failures rather than true alignment. XL-SafetyBench thus contributes to a more nuanced understanding of LLM safety in a multilingual context.
本研究解决了现有大型语言模型（LLM）安全基准的局限性，这些基准主要集中在英语上，往往忽视了特定国家的危害和文化敏感性。以往的方法过于依赖翻译，未能充分评估模型检测文化嵌入问题的能力。提出的XL-SafetyBench引入了一个包含5500个测试案例的综合套件，涵盖10个国家-语言对，采用多阶段管道构建测试项目，包括LLM辅助发现和母语者验证。这种方法允许对模型安全性和文化敏感性进行更细致的评估。该方法使用攻击成功率（ASR）、中性安全率（NSR）和文化敏感性率（CSR）来评估模型，发现前沿模型的越狱鲁棒性和文化意识之间并不一定相关，而本地模型则表现出ASR和NSR之间显著的权衡关系。这些发现支持在多语言LLM背景下进行更详细的跨文化安全评估的必要性。
The Geopolitics of AI Safety: A Causal Analysis of Regional LLM Bias
Authors: Alif Al Hasan
First: 2026-05-06T20:35:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-06T20:35:57+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As Large Language Models (LLMs) are integrated into global software systems, ensuring equitable safety guardrails is a critical requirement. Current fairness evaluations predominantly measure bias observationally, a methodology confounded by the inherent toxicity of topics naturally paired with specific demographics in testing datasets. This study introduces a Probabilistic Graphical Model (PGM) framework to audit LLM safety mechanisms causally. By applying Pearl's do-operator, we mathematically isolate the causal effect of injecting a cultural demographic into a prompt. We conduct a large-scale empirical analysis across seven instruction-tuned models spanning diverse origins: the United States (Llama-3.1-8B, Gemma-2-9B), Europe (Mistral-7B-v0.3), the UAE (Falcon3-7B), China (Qwen2.5-7B, DeepSeek-7B), and India (Airavata-7B). Utilizing two distinct datasets (ToxiGen and BOLD), the findings reveal a disparity between observational and interventional bias, demonstrating that standard fairness metrics can overestimate demographic bias by failing to account for context toxicity. Furthermore, the causal probabilities indicate distinct alignment trends: Western models exhibit higher causal refusal rates for specific demographic groups, whereas Eastern models demonstrate low overall intervention rates with targeted sensitivities toward regional demographics. We discuss the implications of these biases, highlighting how demographic-sensitive over-triggering restricts benign discourse in downstream applications.
中文标题/摘要
标题：人工智能安全的地缘政治：区域大型语言模型偏见的因果分析
随着大型语言模型（LLMs）被整合到全球软件系统中，确保公平的安全防护措施成为一项关键要求。目前的公平性评估主要通过观察性方法测量偏见，这种方法受到测试数据集中与特定人口统计学自然配对的主题固有毒性的干扰。本研究引入了一种概率图模型（PGM）框架，以因果方式审计LLM安全机制。通过应用Pearl的do-操作符，我们在数学上隔离了将文化人口统计学注入提示的因果效应。我们对七个经过指令调优的模型进行了大规模实证分析，这些模型来自不同地区：美国（Llama-3.1-8B，Gemma-2-9B）、欧洲（Mistral-7B-v0.3）、阿联酋（Falcon3-7B）、中国（Qwen2.5-7B，DeepSeek-7B）和印度（Airavata-7B）。利用两个不同的数据集（ToxiGen和BOLD），研究结果揭示了观察性偏见和干预性偏见之间的差异，表明标准公平性指标可能会高估人口统计学偏见，因为未能考虑上下文毒性。此外，因果概率表明了不同的对齐趋势：西方模型对特定人口群体的因果拒绝率较高，而东方模型则表现出较低的整体干预率，并对区域人口统计学具有针对性的敏感性。我们讨论了这些偏见的影响，强调了人口统计学敏感的过度触发如何限制下游应用中的良性讨论。
Summary / 总结
This article addresses the pressing need for equitable safety measures in Large Language Models (LLMs) as they become integral to global software systems. Previous methods primarily relied on observational bias evaluations, which are flawed due to the toxic nature of certain topics associated with specific demographics in testing datasets. The proposed approach introduces a Probabilistic Graphical Model (PGM) framework that utilizes Pearl's do-operator to causally audit LLM safety mechanisms, effectively isolating the impact of cultural demographics in prompts. The study contributes to the understanding of bias in LLMs by revealing significant discrepancies between observational and interventional bias through a large-scale analysis of seven instruction-tuned models from various regions, using two datasets. The findings indicate that standard fairness metrics may overestimate demographic bias, with Western models showing higher refusal rates for certain demographics compared to Eastern models, which exhibit lower intervention rates but heightened sensitivity to regional demographics, thus emphasizing the need for context-aware evaluations in AI safety.
本文探讨了在大型语言模型（LLMs）日益融入全球软件系统的背景下，确保公平安全措施的迫切需求。以往的公平性评估方法主要依赖于观察性偏差评估，这种方法由于测试数据集中某些主题与特定人群固有的毒性而存在缺陷。提出的方法利用概率图模型（PGM）框架对LLM安全机制进行因果审计，通过Pearl的do-operator有效隔离提示中人口统计因素的因果效应。该研究的贡献在于揭示了观察性偏差与干预性偏差之间的显著差异，表明传统的公平性指标可能因上下文毒性而高估人口统计偏差。通过对来自不同地区的七个指令调优模型进行的实证分析，使用两个数据集，结果显示西方模型在特定人群中具有更高的因果拒绝率，而东方模型则表现出较低的干预率，但对区域人口统计具有更高的敏感性，从而强调了在LLM应用中进行上下文敏感偏差评估的必要性。
Safety and accuracy follow different scaling laws in clinical large language models
Authors: Sebastian Wind, Tri-Thien Nguyen, Jeta Sopa, Mahshad Lotfinia, Sebastian Bickelhaup, Michael Uder, Harald Köstler, Gerhard Wellein, Sven Nebelung, Daniel Truhn, Andreas Maier, Soroosh Tayebi Arasteh
First: 2026-05-05T17:57:19+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T17:57:19+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Clinical LLMs are often scaled by increasing model size, context length, retrieval complexity, or inference-time compute, with the implicit expectation that higher accuracy implies safer behavior. This assumption is incomplete in medicine, where a few confident, high-risk, or evidence-contradicting errors can matter more than average benchmark performance. We introduce SaFE-Scale, a framework for measuring how clinical LLM safety changes across model scale, evidence quality, retrieval strategy, context exposure, and inference-time compute. To instantiate this framework, we introduce RadSaFE-200, a Radiology Safety-Focused Evaluation benchmark of 200 multiple-choice questions with clinician-defined clean evidence, conflict evidence, and option-level labels for high-risk error, unsafe answer, and evidence contradiction. We evaluated 34 locally deployed LLMs across six deployment conditions: closed-book prompting (zero-shot), clean evidence, conflict evidence, standard RAG, agentic RAG, and max-context prompting. Clean evidence produced the strongest improvement, increasing mean accuracy from 73.5% to 94.1%, while reducing high-risk error from 12.0% to 2.6%, contradiction from 12.7% to 2.3%, and dangerous overconfidence from 8.0% to 1.6%. Standard RAG and agentic RAG did not reproduce this safety profile: agentic RAG improved accuracy over standard RAG and reduced contradiction, but high-risk error and dangerous overconfidence remained elevated. Max-context prompting increased latency without closing the safety gap, and additional inference-time compute produced only limited gains. Worst-case analysis showed that clinically consequential errors concentrated in a small subset of questions. Clinical LLM safety is therefore not a passive consequence of scaling, but a deployment property shaped by evidence quality, retrieval design, context construction, and collective failure behavior.
中文标题/摘要
标题：临床大型语言模型中的安全性和准确性遵循不同的缩放法则
临床LLM通常通过增加模型大小、上下文长度、检索复杂性或推理时计算来进行缩放，隐含的期望是更高的准确性意味着更安全的行为。这个假设在医学中是不完整的，因为少数自信的高风险或与证据相矛盾的错误可能比平均基准表现更为重要。我们引入了SaFE-Scale，一个测量临床LLM安全性如何随模型规模、证据质量、检索策略、上下文暴露和推理时计算变化的框架。为了实现这个框架，我们引入了RadSaFE-200，这是一个以放射学安全为重点的评估基准，包含200个多项选择题，具有临床医生定义的干净证据、冲突证据和高风险错误、不安全答案及证据矛盾的选项级标签。我们在六种部署条件下评估了34个本地部署的LLM：闭卷提示（零-shot）、干净证据、冲突证据、标准RAG、代理RAG和最大上下文提示。干净证据产生了最强的改进，将平均准确率从73.5%提高到94.1%，同时将高风险错误从12.0%降低到2.6%，矛盾从12.7%降低到2.3%，危险的过度自信从8.0%降低到1.6%。标准RAG和代理RAG未能重现这一安全特征：代理RAG提高了准确性并减少了矛盾，但高风险错误和危险的过度自信仍然较高。最大上下文提示增加了延迟而未缩小安全差距，额外的推理时计算仅产生有限的收益。最坏情况分析显示，临床相关错误集中在少数问题上。因此，临床LLM的安全性并不是缩放的被动结果，而是由证据质量、检索设计、上下文构建和集体失败行为塑造的部署属性。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the inadequacy of existing methods that assume higher accuracy in clinical large language models (LLMs) correlates with safer behavior, particularly in medical contexts where high-risk errors can have significant consequences. The proposed SaFE-Scale framework measures how safety in clinical LLMs varies with model scale, evidence quality, retrieval strategy, context exposure, and inference-time compute, distinguishing it from traditional approaches. The paper introduces RadSaFE-200, a benchmark designed to evaluate safety-focused performance through multiple-choice questions that assess high-risk errors and evidence contradictions. The methodology involved evaluating 34 LLMs under various deployment conditions, revealing that using clean evidence significantly improved accuracy from 73.5% to 94.1% while reducing high-risk errors and contradictions. These findings indicate that safety in clinical LLMs is influenced by deployment factors rather than merely model scaling, highlighting the need for careful consideration of evidence quality and retrieval design in clinical applications.
本研究解决了现有方法的不足，即假设临床大型语言模型（LLMs）的更高准确性与更安全的行为相关，这在医学背景下尤其成问题，因为少数关键错误可能产生重大后果。提出的SaFE-Scale框架测量临床LLMs的安全性如何随着模型规模、证据质量、检索策略、上下文暴露和推理时间计算而变化，这与过去主要关注准确性的做法形成对比。本文引入了RadSaFE-200基准，由200个多项选择题组成，旨在评估LLMs的安全相关方面，并在各种部署条件下评估了34个LLMs。结果表明，使用干净证据显著提高了准确性，从73.5%提高到94.1%，同时减少了高风险错误和矛盾，突显出安全性受多种因素影响，而不仅仅是模型规模。该研究通过表明安全性是由部署策略塑造的复杂属性，而不是模型规模或复杂性增加的直接结果，贡献了对临床环境中LLMs安全性的理解。
Exposing LLM Safety Gaps Through Mathematical Encoding:New Attacks and Systematic Analysis
Authors: Haoyu Zhang, Mohammad Zandsalimy, Shanu Sushmita
First: 2026-05-05T07:25:33+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-05T07:25:33+00:00
Comments: 16 pages, 2 figures, 4 tables. Accepted as a long paper at the 39th Canadian Conference on Artificial Intelligence (Canadian AI 2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Large language models (LLMs) employ safety mechanisms to prevent harmful outputs, yet these defenses primarily rely on semantic pattern matching. We show that encoding harmful prompts as coherent mathematical problems -- using formalisms such as set theory, formal logic, and quantum mechanics -- bypasses these filters at high rates, achieving 46%--56% average attack success across eight target models and two established benchmarks. Crucially, the effectiveness depends not on mathematical notation itself, but on whether a helper LLM deeply reformulates the harmful content into a genuine mathematical problem: rule-based encodings that apply mathematical formatting without such reformulation perform no better than unencoded baselines. We introduce a novel Formal Logic encoding that achieves attack success comparable to Set Theory, demonstrating that this vulnerability generalizes across mathematical formalisms. Additional experiments with repeat post-processing confirm that these attacks are robust to simple prompt augmentation. Notably, newer models (GPT-5, GPT-5-Mini) show substantially greater robustness than older models, though they remain vulnerable. Our findings highlight fundamental gaps in current safety frameworks and motivate defenses that reason about mathematical structure rather than surface-level semantics.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过数学编码揭示大型语言模型的安全漏洞：新攻击与系统分析
大型语言模型（LLMs）采用安全机制以防止有害输出，但这些防御主要依赖于语义模式匹配。我们展示了将有害提示编码为连贯的数学问题——使用集合论、形式逻辑和量子力学等形式——可以高效绕过这些过滤器，在八个目标模型和两个已建立基准上实现46%至56%的平均攻击成功率。关键在于，效果并不依赖于数学符号本身，而在于辅助LLM是否将有害内容深度重构为真正的数学问题：仅应用数学格式的基于规则的编码表现与未编码基线无异。我们引入了一种新颖的形式逻辑编码，其攻击成功率与集合论相当，表明这种脆弱性在数学形式中具有普遍性。对重复后处理的额外实验确认这些攻击对简单提示增强具有鲁棒性。值得注意的是，较新的模型（GPT-5，GPT-5-Mini）显示出比旧模型更大的鲁棒性，尽管它们仍然脆弱。我们的发现突显了当前安全框架中的基本缺口，并激励针对数学结构而非表面语义进行推理的防御措施。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the limitations of current safety mechanisms in large language models (LLMs), which primarily rely on semantic pattern matching to prevent harmful outputs. Previous methods have struggled with bypassing these defenses, and the proposed approach introduces a novel encoding of harmful prompts as coherent mathematical problems using formal systems like set theory and formal logic. This method effectively exposes vulnerabilities in LLMs, achieving an average attack success rate of 46% to 56% across eight models and two benchmarks, demonstrating that the key factor is the deep reformulation of harmful content into genuine mathematical problems rather than merely applying mathematical notation. The paper contributes by revealing significant gaps in existing safety frameworks and suggesting that future defenses should focus on the mathematical structure of prompts. The methodology includes systematic analysis and experimentation with various mathematical encodings, showing that even newer models remain vulnerable despite improved robustness.
本研究针对当前大型语言模型（LLMs）安全机制的局限性进行探讨，这些机制主要依赖语义模式匹配来防止有害输出。以往的方法在有效编码有害提示方面存在困难，导致了漏洞，而所提出的方法旨在通过将这些提示重新表述为连贯的数学问题来利用这些漏洞，使用如集合论等形式逻辑。本文贡献了一种新颖的形式逻辑编码方法，在八个目标模型中实现了46%到56%的攻击成功率，表明这些攻击的有效性依赖于深度重构，而不仅仅是数学格式化。该方法论涉及对各种数学形式的系统分析和实验，揭示了较新模型表现出更大的鲁棒性，但仍然存在脆弱性。这些发现强调了现有安全框架中的重大缺口，并建议需要关注提示的数学结构而不仅仅是其语义内容的防御措施。
From Prompt to Physical Actuation: Holistic Threat Modeling of LLM-Enabled Robotic Systems
Authors: Neha Nagaraja, Hayretdin Bahsi, Carlo R. da Cunha
First: 2026-04-29T23:44:07+00:00 · Latest: 2026-05-04T05:54:12+00:00
Comments: Submitted to 23rd Annual International Conference on Privacy, Security, and Trust (PST2026)
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large language models are integrated into autonomous robotic systems for task planning and control, compromised inputs or unsafe model outputs can propagate through the planning pipeline to physical-world consequences. Although prior work has studied robotic cybersecurity, adversarial perception attacks, and LLM safety independently, no existing study traces how these threat categories interact and propagate across trust boundaries in a unified architectural model. We address this gap by modeling an LLM-enabled autonomous robot in an edge-cloud architecture as a hierarchical Data Flow Diagram and applying STRIDE-per-interaction analysis across six boundary-crossing interaction points using a three-category taxonomy of Conventional Cyber Threats, Adversarial Threats, and Conversational Threats. The analysis reveals that these categories converge at the same boundary crossings, and we trace three cross-boundary attack chains from external entry points to unsafe physical actuation, each exposing a distinct architectural property: the absence of independent semantic validation between user input and actuator dispatch, cross-modal translation from visual perception to language-model instruction, and unmediated boundary crossing through provider-side tool use. To our knowledge, this is the first DFD-based threat analysis integrating all three threat categories across the full perception-planning-actuation pipeline of an LLM-enabled robotic system.
中文标题/摘要
标题：从提示到物理执行：LLM驱动机器人系统的整体威胁建模
随着大型语言模型被集成到自主机器人系统中进行任务规划和控制，受损的输入或不安全的模型输出可能会通过规划流程传播到物理世界的后果。尽管之前的研究独立地研究了机器人网络安全、对抗性感知攻击和LLM安全，但尚无现有研究追踪这些威胁类别如何在统一的架构模型中相互作用和传播。我们通过将LLM驱动的自主机器人建模为边缘-云架构中的分层数据流图，并在六个跨边界交互点应用基于交互的STRIDE分析，使用常规网络威胁、对抗性威胁和对话威胁的三类分类法来填补这一空白。分析表明，这些类别在相同的边界交叉处汇聚，我们追踪了三条跨边界攻击链，从外部入口点到不安全的物理执行，每条链暴露出一个独特的架构特性：用户输入与执行器调度之间缺乏独立的语义验证、从视觉感知到语言模型指令的跨模态翻译，以及通过提供方工具使用的无中介边界跨越。据我们所知，这是首个基于DFD的威胁分析，整合了所有三类威胁，涵盖了LLM驱动机器人系统的完整感知-规划-执行流程。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the critical issue of safety in LLM-enabled autonomous robotic systems, where compromised inputs or unsafe outputs can lead to real-world consequences. Previous studies have examined aspects of robotic cybersecurity, adversarial perception attacks, and LLM safety in isolation, failing to explore the interactions and propagation of these threats across trust boundaries. This paper proposes a unified architectural model using a hierarchical Data Flow Diagram (DFD) and applies STRIDE-per-interaction analysis to six boundary-crossing interaction points, revealing how Conventional Cyber Threats, Adversarial Threats, and Conversational Threats converge. The findings highlight three distinct attack chains that expose vulnerabilities in the system, such as the lack of semantic validation and unmediated boundary crossings. This work contributes a comprehensive threat analysis framework that integrates multiple threat categories across the perception-planning-actuation pipeline, marking a significant advancement in understanding the security implications of LLM integration in robotics.
本研究关注大型语言模型（LLM）在自主机器人系统中的应用，强调了被破坏的输入和不安全输出可能导致物理世界后果的风险。以往的研究分别考察了机器人网络安全和对抗性攻击，未能考虑这些威胁如何在信任边界上相互作用。本文提出了一种统一的威胁建模方法，使用分层数据流图（DFD）和每个交互的STRIDE分析，识别六个交互点的脆弱性，揭示传统、对抗和对话威胁在这些边界处汇聚。研究结果暴露了关键的架构弱点，如缺乏语义验证和无中介的边界穿越，标志着这是对LLM启用的机器人系统在整个感知-规划-执行管道中进行的首次全面威胁分析，从而对机器人网络安全领域做出了重要贡献。
Useless but Safe? Benchmarking Utility Recovery with User Intent Clarification in Multi-Turn Conversations
Authors: Mingqian Zheng, Malia Morgan, Liwei Jiang, Carolyn Rose, Maarten Sap
First: 2026-04-29T18:37:18+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-29T18:37:18+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Current LLM safety alignment techniques improve model robustness against adversarial attacks, but overlook whether and how LLMs can recover helpfulness when benign users clarify their intent. We introduce CarryOnBench, the first interactive benchmark that measures whether LLMs can revise their interpretation of user intent and recover utility, while remaining safe through multi-turn conversations. Starting from 398 seemingly harmful queries with benign underlying intents, we simulate 5,970 conversations by varying user follow-up sequences, evaluating 14 models on both intent-aligned utility and safety. CarryOnBench yields 1,866 different conversation flows of 4--12 turns, totaling 23,880 model responses. We design Ben-Util, a checklist-based metric that evaluates how well each model response fulfills the user's benign information need using atomic items. At turn one, models fulfill only 10.5--37.6% of the user's benign information need. When the same query includes the benign intent upfront, models fulfill 25.1--72.1%, confirming that models withhold information due to intent misinterpretation, not limited knowledge. With benign clarifications in multi-turn conversations, 13 of 14 models approach or exceed this single-turn baseline, yet recovery cost varies across models. We identify three failure modes invisible to single-turn evaluations: utility lock-in, where a model rarely updates despite clarification; unsafe recovery, where a model updates at disproportionate safety cost; and repetitive recovery, where a model recycles prior responses rather than providing new information. Moreover, conversations converge to similar harmfulness levels regardless of how conservative the model starts. These findings expose a gap that single-turn evaluations miss -- whether a model is appropriately cautious or simply unresponsive to clarified user intent.
中文标题/摘要
标题：无用但安全？在多轮对话中通过用户意图澄清基准测试实用性恢复
当前的LLM安全对齐技术提高了模型对抗攻击的鲁棒性，但忽视了LLM在良性用户澄清意图时是否以及如何恢复有用性。我们引入CarryOnBench，这是第一个交互式基准，测量LLM在多轮对话中是否能够修正对用户意图的解释并恢复实用性，同时保持安全。从398个看似有害的查询开始，这些查询具有良性的潜在意图，我们通过变化用户后续序列模拟了5,970个对话，评估了14个模型在意图对齐的实用性和安全性方面的表现。CarryOnBench产生了1,866种不同的对话流程，轮次为4到12，总计23,880个模型响应。我们设计了Ben-Util，这是一个基于清单的指标，评估每个模型响应在多大程度上满足用户的良性信息需求。在第一轮中，模型仅满足用户良性信息需求的10.5%到37.6%。当同一查询在前面包含良性意图时，模型满足25.1%到72.1%，确认模型因意图误解而隐瞒信息，而不是知识有限。在多轮对话中，经过良性澄清，14个模型中有13个接近或超过这一单轮基准，但恢复成本在模型之间有所不同。我们识别出三种在单轮评估中不可见的失败模式：实用性锁定，即模型在澄清后很少更新；不安全恢复，即模型以不成比例的安全成本进行更新；以及重复恢复，即模型回收先前的响应而不是提供新信息。此外，无论模型起初多么保守，对话都趋向于相似的有害性水平。这些发现揭示了单轮评估所忽视的一个差距——模型是否适当地谨慎，或仅仅对澄清的用户意图无反应。
Summary / 总结
This research addresses the limitations of current large language model (LLM) safety alignment techniques, which enhance robustness against adversarial attacks but fail to assess the models' ability to recover helpfulness when users clarify their intent in multi-turn conversations. Previous methods primarily focused on single-turn evaluations, overlooking the dynamics of user intent clarification, leading to issues such as utility lock-in and unsafe recovery. The proposed approach, CarryOnBench, introduces an interactive benchmark that simulates 5,970 conversations to evaluate 14 models on their ability to align with user intent while maintaining safety. The study reveals that models initially fulfill only a fraction of benign information needs, but with clarifications, many models improve their performance, highlighting the importance of multi-turn interactions. The findings indicate that single-turn evaluations miss critical failure modes, thus contributing to a deeper understanding of LLM behavior in conversational contexts.
本研究解决了当前大型语言模型（LLM）安全对齐技术的局限性，这些技术增强了对抗攻击的鲁棒性，但未能评估模型在用户澄清意图时恢复有用性的能力，尤其是在多轮对话中。以往的方法主要集中在单轮评估，忽视了用户意图澄清的动态变化，这可能导致误解和效用降低。提出的方法CarryOnBench引入了一个互动基准，评估LLM在保持安全的同时修正用户意图理解的能力。该方法通过模拟基于398个有害查询的5970个对话，评估14个模型在满足用户需求和确保安全方面的表现。研究结果表明，在第一轮中，模型仅满足10.5%-37.6%的良性信息需求，但在澄清后，14个模型中有13个提高了性能，突显了意图澄清在增强模型效用中的重要性。此外，研究还识别了单轮评估所忽视的失败模式，如效用锁定和不安全恢复，从而为LLM在对话上下文中的评估提供了有价值的见解。
Policy-Grounded Safety Evaluation of 20 Large Language Models
Authors: Juan Manuel Contreras
First: 2025-07-19T18:49:16+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-29T15:54:46+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
As large language models (LLMs) become increasingly integrated into real-world applications, scalable and rigorous safety evaluation is essential. This paper introduces Aymara AI, a programmatic platform for generating and administering customized, policy-grounded safety evaluations. Aymara AI transforms natural-language safety policies into adversarial prompts and scores model responses using an AI-based rater validated against human judgments. We demonstrate its capabilities through the Aymara LLM Risk and Responsibility Matrix, which evaluates 20 commercially available LLMs across 10 real-world safety domains. Results reveal wide performance disparities, with mean safety scores ranging from 86.2% to 52.4%. While models performed well in well-established safety domains such as Misinformation (mean = 95.7%), they consistently failed in more complex or underspecified domains, notably Privacy & Impersonation (mean = 24.3%). Analyses of Variance confirmed that safety scores differed significantly across both models and domains (p < .05). These findings underscore the inconsistent and context-dependent nature of LLM safety and highlight the need for scalable, customizable tools like Aymara AI to support responsible AI development and oversight.
中文标题/摘要
标题：基于政策的20个大型语言模型的安全评估
随着大型语言模型（LLMs）越来越多地融入现实应用，规模化和严格的安全评估变得至关重要。本文介绍了Aymara AI，一个用于生成和管理定制化、基于政策的安全评估的程序化平台。Aymara AI将自然语言安全政策转化为对抗性提示，并使用经过人类判断验证的基于AI的评分者对模型响应进行评分。我们通过Aymara LLM风险与责任矩阵展示其能力，该矩阵评估了20个商业可用的LLM在10个现实安全领域的表现。结果显示，性能差异显著，平均安全评分范围从86.2%到52.4%。虽然模型在虚假信息等成熟安全领域表现良好（平均=95.7%），但在更复杂或不明确的领域（特别是隐私与冒充）中表现不佳（平均=24.3%）。方差分析确认，安全评分在模型和领域之间存在显著差异（p < .05）。这些发现强调了LLM安全性的不一致性和依赖于上下文的特性，并突显了像Aymara AI这样的可扩展、可定制工具在支持负责任的AI开发和监督中的必要性。
Summary / 总结
The research addresses the growing need for effective safety evaluations of large language models (LLMs) as they are increasingly used in real-world applications. Previous methods lacked scalability and rigor, often failing to provide comprehensive assessments across diverse safety domains. The proposed Aymara AI platform offers a novel approach by converting natural-language safety policies into adversarial prompts and evaluating model responses with an AI-based rater, which is validated against human judgments. This method effectively addresses the limitations of existing evaluations by providing customizable and context-aware assessments. The paper contributes by demonstrating the capabilities of Aymara AI through the evaluation of 20 LLMs across 10 safety domains, revealing significant performance disparities, with scores ranging from 86.2% to 52.4%, and highlighting the models' weaknesses in complex domains like Privacy & Impersonation, thus supporting the need for improved safety evaluation tools.

Evaluating LLM Safety Under Repeated Inference via Accelerated Prompt Stress Testing
Authors: Keita Broadwater
First: 2026-02-12T10:09:13+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-28T16:38:37+00:00
Comments: 23 pages, 9 figures; editorial and LaTeX revisions for clarity; improved presentation of methodology and results; updated figures, tables, and float placement; clarified temperature sensitivity and deployment-risk analysis; expanded reporting from the same experiments; results unchanged in substance
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Traditional benchmarks for large language models (LLMs), such as HELM and AIR-BENCH, primarily assess safety through breadth-oriented evaluation across diverse tasks and risk categories. However, real-world deployment often exposes a different class of risk: operational failures that arise under repeated inference on identical or near-identical prompts rather than from broad task-level underperformance. In high-stakes settings, response consistency and safety under sustained use are therefore critical. We introduce Accelerated Prompt Stress Testing (APST), a depth-oriented evaluation framework inspired by highly accelerated stress testing in reliability engineering. APST repeatedly samples identical prompts under controlled operational conditions (such as decoding temperature) to surface latent failure modes including hallucinations, refusal inconsistency, and unsafe completions. Rather than treating failures as isolated events, APST models them as stochastic outcomes of repeated inference and uses Bernoulli and binomial formulations to estimate per-inference failure probabilities. Applying APST to multiple instruction-tuned LLMs evaluated on AIR-BENCH 2024--derived safety and security prompts, we find that models with comparable shallow-evaluation scores can exhibit substantially different empirical failure rates under repeated sampling. These results show that single-sample or low-depth evaluation can obscure meaningful differences in deployment-relevant reliability. APST complements existing benchmark methodologies by providing a practical framework for estimating failure frequency under sustained use and comparing safety reliability across models and decoding configurations.
中文标题/摘要
标题：通过加速提示压力测试评估大语言模型的安全性
传统的大语言模型（LLMs）基准，如HELM和AIR-BENCH，主要通过在多样任务和风险类别中的广度评估来评估安全性。然而，实际部署往往暴露出另一类风险：在相同或近似相同的提示下重复推理所导致的操作失败，而不是广泛任务级别的表现不佳。在高风险环境中，响应一致性和持续使用下的安全性至关重要。我们引入了加速提示压力测试（APST），这是一个受可靠性工程中高度加速压力测试启发的深度评估框架。APST在受控操作条件下（如解码温度）重复采样相同的提示，以揭示潜在的失败模式，包括幻觉、拒绝不一致和不安全的完成。APST将失败视为重复推理的随机结果，并使用伯努利和二项式公式来估计每次推理的失败概率。将APST应用于多个在AIR-BENCH 2024上评估的指令调优LLMs的安全和安全提示，我们发现具有可比浅层评估分数的模型在重复采样下可能表现出显著不同的经验失败率。这些结果表明，单样本或低深度评估可能掩盖在部署相关可靠性方面的有意义差异。APST通过提供一个实用框架来估计持续使用下的失败频率，并比较模型和解码配置之间的安全可靠性，补充了现有的基准方法。

Adaptive Prompt Embedding Optimization for LLM Jailbreaking
Authors: Miles Q. Li, Benjamin C. M. Fung, Boyang Li, Radin Hamidi Rad, Ebrahim Bagheri
First: 2026-04-27T20:39:08+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-27T20:39:08+00:00
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Existing white-box jailbreak attacks against aligned LLMs typically append discrete adversarial suffixes to the user prompt, which visibly alters the prompt and operates in a combinatorial token space. Prior work has avoided directly optimizing the embeddings of the original prompt tokens, presumably because perturbing them risks destroying the prompt's semantic content. We propose Prompt Embedding Optimization (PEO), a multi-round white-box jailbreak that directly optimizes the embeddings of the original prompt tokens without appending any adversarial tokens, and show that the concern is unfounded: the optimized embeddings remain close enough to their originals that the visible prompt string is preserved exactly after nearest-token projection, and quantitative analysis shows the model's responses stay on topic for the large majority of prompts. PEO combines continuous embedding-space optimization with structured continuation targets and an adaptive failure-focused schedule. Counterintuitively, later PEO rounds can benefit from heuristic composite response scaffolds that are not natural standalone templates, yet ASR-Judge shows that the resulting gains are not merely empty formatting or scaffold-only outputs. Across two standard harmful-behavior benchmarks and competing white-box attacks spanning discrete suffix search, appended adversarial embeddings, and search-based adversarial generation, PEO outperforms all of them in our experiments.
中文标题/摘要
标题：用于大型语言模型越狱的自适应提示嵌入优化
现有针对对齐大型语言模型的白盒越狱攻击通常在用户提示后附加离散的对抗后缀，这明显改变了提示并在组合标记空间中操作。之前的工作避免直接优化原始提示标记的嵌入，可能是因为扰动它们会破坏提示的语义内容。我们提出了提示嵌入优化（PEO），这是一种多轮白盒越狱，直接优化原始提示标记的嵌入，而不附加任何对抗标记，并表明这种担忧是没有根据的：优化后的嵌入与原始嵌入保持足够接近，以至于在最近标记投影后可见的提示字符串完全保留，定量分析表明模型的响应在绝大多数提示中保持主题一致。PEO结合了连续嵌入空间优化、结构化延续目标和自适应失败聚焦调度。出乎意料的是，后期PEO轮次可以受益于并非自然独立模板的启发式复合响应支架，但ASR-Judge显示，所获得的收益不仅仅是空格式或仅支架输出。在两个标准有害行为基准和涵盖离散后缀搜索、附加对抗嵌入和基于搜索的对抗生成的竞争白盒攻击中，PEO在我们的实验中表现优于所有这些方法。

Beyond Context: Large Language Models' Failure to Grasp Users' Intent
Authors: Ahmed M. Hussain, Salahuddin Salahuddin
First: 2025-12-24T11:15:57+00:00 · Latest: 2026-04-24T20:27:34+00:00
Comments: 22 pages and 23 figures; updated authors list and revised manuscript
Abs · PDF · Code1 · Code2
Abstract
Current Large Language Models (LLMs) safety approaches focus on explicitly harmful content while overlooking a critical vulnerability: the inability to understand context and recognize user intent. This creates exploitable vulnerabilities that malicious users can systematically leverage to circumvent safety mechanisms. We empirically evaluate multiple state-of-the-art LLMs, including ChatGPT, Claude, Gemini, and DeepSeek. Our analysis demonstrates the circumvention of reliable safety mechanisms through emotional framing, progressive revelation, and academic justification techniques. Notably, reasoning-enabled configurations amplified rather than mitigated the effectiveness of exploitation, increasing factual precision while failing to interrogate the underlying intent. The exception was Claude Opus 4.1, which prioritized intent detection over information provision in some use cases. This pattern reveals that current architectural designs create systematic vulnerabilities. These limitations require paradigmatic shifts toward contextual understanding and intent recognition as core safety capabilities rather than post-hoc protective mechanisms.
中文标题/摘要
标题：超越上下文：大型语言模型未能理解用户意图
当前大型语言模型（LLMs）的安全方法专注于显性有害内容，而忽视了一个关键漏洞：无法理解上下文和识别用户意图。这导致了恶意用户可以系统性利用的可利用漏洞，从而规避安全机制。我们对多个最先进的LLMs进行了实证评估，包括ChatGPT、Claude、Gemini和DeepSeek。我们的分析表明，通过情感框架、渐进揭示和学术辩护技术，可靠安全机制被规避。值得注意的是，启用推理的配置增强了而不是减轻了利用的有效性，提高了事实精确性，但未能质疑潜在意图。例外是Claude Opus 4.1，在某些用例中优先考虑意图检测而非信息提供。这一模式揭示了当前架构设计造成的系统性漏洞。这些局限性需要在上下文理解和意图识别方面进行范式转变，将其作为核心安全能力，而不是事后保护机制。
